    let open = false;
    $(".cut.icon_menu_right").mouseleave(function () {
        setTimeout(function () {

            if ($('.cut.icon_menu_right:hover').length != 0) {
                return;
            }
           
            if (open) {
                $(".menu-ext").slideUp("slow");
                open = false;

        }, 400);

    });

        .hover(() => {
            open = true;

    }
    
    function expandcollapse(value,industrytype)
    {
    
        if(type == 'BSheet')
        {
            var str = "";
            if(industrytype==1)
            {
                str = value.id.substring(0,2);
            }
            else if(industrytype==2)
            {
                if(value.id == "00111") str = value.id.substring(0,5);
                else str = value.id.substring(0,4);
            }
            if(value.id == "00111")
            {
                if(document.getElementById("001111").style.display == "none")
                {
                    document.getElementById("001111").style.display = "";
                }
                else
                {
                    document.getElementById("001111").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            else
            {            
                for(var i=0;i<list.length;i++)
                {

                    if (list[i] == "001111") {
                    }
                    else {
                        if (list[i].indexOf(str) == 0 || (industrytype == 1 && ((str=="31" && list[i].indexOf("32")==0)||(str=="41" && list[i].indexOf("42")==0) || (str=="33" && list[i].indexOf("34")==0)))) {
                            if (list[i] == "001111")
                            { }
                            else if (list[i] == "00111")
                            { }
                            else if (list[i] == "0011")
                            { }
                            else {
                                if (document.getElementById(list[i]).style.display == "none") {
                                    document.getElementById(list[i]).style.display = "";
                                }
                                else {
                                    document.getElementById(list[i]).style.display = "none";
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            document.getElementById(value.id).style.display = "";
            if (document.getElementById('img_' + value.id).src == "https://cafef1.mediacdn.vn//batdongsan/Images/media/plusi.gif")
            {                
                document.getElementById('img_' + value.id).src = "https://cafef1.mediacdn.vn//batdongsan/Images/media/minus.gif"
            }
            else
            {                
                document.getElementById('img_' + value.id).src = "https://cafef1.mediacdn.vn//batdongsan/Images/media/plusi.gif"
            }
        }
    }
    
    function redirectBc(sym, type, year, quarter, showtype, idx)
    {
        var uname = '';
        var stype = 'bao-cao-tai-chinh';
        window.location = "/bao-cao-tai-chinh/" + sym + "/" + type + "/" + year + "/" + quarter + "/" + idx + "/" + showtype + "/" + stype + "-" + uname + ".chn";
    }

    function redirectBc2(sym, type, year, quarter, showtype, idx,option) {
        var uname = '';
        var stype = 'bao-cao-tai-chinh';
        window.location = "/bao-cao-tai-chinh/" + sym + "/" + type + "/" + year + "/" + quarter + "/" + idx + "/" + showtype + "/" + option + "/" + stype + "-" + uname + ".chn";
    }
    
    function redirectShowType(showtype)
    {
        redirectBc2(sym,type,nam,quy,showtype,idx,option);
    }
    
    function redirectFromSelect(quy)
    {   
        redirectBc(sym,type,nam,quy,'0',0);
    }
    function redirectFromSelect2(quy,option) {
        redirectBc2(sym, type, nam, quy, '0', 0,option);
    }
    function redirectFromSearch()
    {
        
        var sym = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolder1_txtKeyword').value;
        var quy = "1";
        if(sym == "")
        {
            alert('Ban chua chon ma co phieu!');
        }
        else
        {
            redirectBc(sym,type,nam,quy,'0',0);
        }

    }
    
    function redirectBCTC(type)
    {
        //var sym = 'tta';
        //var quy = '2';
        //var nam = '2024';
        redirectBc(sym,type,nam,quy,'0',0);
    }
    
    function reNext()
    {
        //var sym = 'tta';
        //var type = 'bsheet';
        quy = '2';
        //var nam = '2024';
        idx = idx - 1;
        if(quy != 0)
        {
            if(quy == 4)
            {
                quy = 1;
                nam = parseInt(nam) + 1;
            }
            else
                quy = parseInt(quy) + 1;
                
            redirectBc(sym,type,nam,quy,'0',idx);
        }
        else
        {
            nam = parseInt(nam) + 1;
            redirectBc(sym,type,nam,0,'0',idx);
        }
    }
    
    function rePre()
    {
        var sym = 'tta';
        var type = 'bsheet';
        quy = '2';
        idx = parseInt(idx) + 1;
        //var nam = '2024';
        if(quy != 0)
        {
            if(quy == 1)
            {
                quy = 4;
                nam = parseInt(nam) - 1;
            }
            else
                quy = parseInt(quy) - 1;
                
            redirectBc(sym,type,nam,quy,'0',idx);
        }
        else
        {
            nam = parseInt(nam) - 1;
            redirectBc(sym,type,nam,0,'0', idx);
        }
    }    
</script>

        $(document).ready(function () {
            $("#back-top").hide();
            $(function () {
                $(window).scroll(function () {
                    if ($(this).scrollTop() > 500) {
                        $('#scroll_top').fadeIn();
                    } else {
                        $('#scroll_top').fadeOut();
                    }
                    if ($(this).scrollTop() > 210) {
                        $('#menuv3').css("position", "fixed").css("top", "0").css("box-shadow", "0 2px 4px #333");
                    }
                    else {
                        $('#menuv3').css("position", "relative").css("box-shadow", "none");
                    }
                });
                $('#scroll_top').click(function () {
                    $('body,html').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 800);
                    return false;
                });
            });
        });
    </script>
